<p>I get so excited for asparagus season every year! Not only are they <em>way</em> less expensive when in season, but theyâre also just <em>so</em> much more delicious. And because the price is just so inflated the rest of the year, I pretty much save all my asparagus eating for the spring, when theyâre in season. This simple method for Lemon Garlic Roasted Asparagus is one of the easiest ways to prepare asparagus and itâs so scrumptious that I could just about eat the entire bunch myself. Consider that a fair warning. ;)  </p>
<span id="more-13342"></span>
<p><em>Originally posted 3/5/2011, updated 4/16/2021.</em></p>

<h2>Why I Love Roasted Asparagus</h2>
<p>There are several ways to cook asparagus, but roasting takes first prize for me. Roasting kind of concentrates the flavor, so you get a much more deep, savory flavor than lighter cooking methods like steaming or sautÃ©ing. The edges get a little brown and crispy, which gives them so much wonderful texture. Theyâre just a delight to eat. </p>
<h2>When is Asparagus Season?</h2>
<p>As I mentioned in the introduction, asparagus is definitely one of those vegetables that you want to buy in season to get the best price and flavor. Asparagus are in season during the spring months, or from late February to early June, depending on where you live. </p>
<h2>How to Pick Good Asparagus</h2>
<p>Avoid choosing asparagus that arenât kept moist at the grocery store. Check the cut ends to make sure theyâre not dry (even better if theyâre displayed with cut ends in water), and make sure the asparagus itself is crisp and not soft or rubbery. The flowering end should be tightly closed to the stalk.</p>
<h2>What to Serve with Lemon Garlic Roasted Asparagus</h2>
<p> Lemon Garlic Roasted Asparagus are a classic, simple side dish for roasted or grilled meats. These asparagus would go great with <a href="https://www.budgetbytes.com/easy-lemon-pepper-chicken/">Lemon Pepper Chicken</a>, <a href="https://www.budgetbytes.com/brown-sugar-roasted-pork-loin/">Brown Sugar Roasted Pork Loin</a>, <a href="https://www.budgetbytes.com/honey-mustard-pork-chops/">Honey Mustard Pork Chops</a>, or <a href="https://www.budgetbytes.com/creamy-mushroom-chicken-with-crispy-onions/">Creamy Mushroom Chicken with Crispy Onions</a>. You might also want to make some <a href="https://www.budgetbytes.com/easy-hollandaise-sauce/">Hollandaise Sauce</a> to drizzle over these delicious asparagus!</p>

<div class="wprm-recipe-instructions-container wprm-recipe-54829-instructions-container wprm-block-text-normal" data-recipe="54829"><h3 class="wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-instructions-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none" style="">Instructions</h3><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group"><ul class="wprm-recipe-instructions"><li class="wprm-recipe-instruction" id="wprm-recipe-54829-step-0-0" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><span style="display: block;">Preheat the oven to 400ÂºF. Rinse the asparagus well, then trim off the dry or woody end of the stem (usually about one inch needs to be removed from the ends). Mince two cloves of garlic.</span></div></li><li class="wprm-recipe-instruction" id="wprm-recipe-54829-step-0-1" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><span style="display: block;">Line a baking sheet with parchment paper for easy cleanup, if desired. Place the trimmed asparagus on the baking sheet along with the minced garlic. Drizzle the olive oil over top, then add the salt and pepper. Toss the asparagus until they are coated in garlic, oil, salt, and pepper.</span></div></li><li class="wprm-recipe-instruction" id="wprm-recipe-54829-step-0-2" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><span style="display: block;">Transfer the asparagus to the preheated 400ÂºF oven and roast for 20 minutes or until they have browned to your liking (roasting time may vary depending on the girth of your asparagus). Stir once halfway through roasting.</span></div></li><li class="wprm-recipe-instruction" id="wprm-recipe-54829-step-0-3" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><span style="display: block;">While the asparagus are cooking, zest the lemon using the fine side of a box grater or a small-holed cheese grater. You'll need about 1 tsp zest. After zesting, cut the lemon into wedges.</span></div></li><li class="wprm-recipe-instruction" id="wprm-recipe-54829-step-0-4" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><span style="display: block;">Once the asparagus are roasted, add the lemon zest and a couple squeezes of lemon juice. Toss to coat. Taste and adjust the salt or lemon as desired. Serve with the remaining lemon wedges. </span></div></li></ul></div></div>

<h2>How to Make Lemon Garlic Roasted Asparagus â Step by Step Photos</h2>
<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img alt="Ends trimmed off asparagus" class="wp-image-54831" data-loading="lazy" data-pin-media="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/1-Trim-Asparagus.jpg" data-src="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/1-Trim-Asparagus.jpg" data-srcset="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/1-Trim-Asparagus.jpg 1200w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/1-Trim-Asparagus-400x300.jpg 400w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/1-Trim-Asparagus-800x600.jpg 800w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/1-Trim-Asparagus-347x260.jpg 347w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/1-Trim-Asparagus-768x576.jpg 768w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/1-Trim-Asparagus-115x86.jpg 115w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/1-Trim-Asparagus-693x520.jpg 693w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/1-Trim-Asparagus-391x293.jpg 391w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/1-Trim-Asparagus-227x170.jpg 227w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/1-Trim-Asparagus-500x375.jpg 500w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/1-Trim-Asparagus-853x640.jpg 853w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/1-Trim-Asparagus-150x113.jpg 150w" height="900" sizes="(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAP///wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw==" width="1200"/></figure>
<p><em>Preheat the oven to 400ÂºF. Rinse one bunch of asparagus (about 1 lb.), then trim off the dry woody ends. Sometimes I leave the rubber bands on while trimming to make it a bit easier. Mince two cloves of garlic.</em></p>
<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img alt="asparagus, garlic, oil, and salt on a baking sheet" class="wp-image-54832" data-loading="lazy" data-pin-media="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/2-Season-Asparagus.jpg" data-src="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/2-Season-Asparagus.jpg" data-srcset="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/2-Season-Asparagus.jpg 1200w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/2-Season-Asparagus-400x300.jpg 400w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/2-Season-Asparagus-800x600.jpg 800w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/2-Season-Asparagus-347x260.jpg 347w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/2-Season-Asparagus-768x576.jpg 768w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/2-Season-Asparagus-115x86.jpg 115w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/2-Season-Asparagus-693x520.jpg 693w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/2-Season-Asparagus-391x293.jpg 391w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/2-Season-Asparagus-227x170.jpg 227w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/2-Season-Asparagus-500x375.jpg 500w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/2-Season-Asparagus-853x640.jpg 853w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/2-Season-Asparagus-150x113.jpg 150w" height="900" sizes="(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAP///wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw==" width="1200"/></figure>
<p><em>Line a baking sheet with parchment paper, if you prefer easy cleanup. Add the trimmed asparagus to the baking sheet along with the minced garlic, 1 Tbsp olive oil, and about 1/8 tsp salt and pepper. Toss the asparagus until theyâre coated in oil, garlic, salt, and pepper. Transfer to the oven to roast.</em></p>
<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img alt="Zested lemon on a cutting board with a small-holed cheese grater" class="wp-image-54833" data-loading="lazy" data-pin-media="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/3-Lemon-Zest.jpg" data-src="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/3-Lemon-Zest.jpg" data-srcset="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/3-Lemon-Zest.jpg 1200w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/3-Lemon-Zest-400x300.jpg 400w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/3-Lemon-Zest-800x600.jpg 800w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/3-Lemon-Zest-347x260.jpg 347w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/3-Lemon-Zest-768x576.jpg 768w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/3-Lemon-Zest-115x86.jpg 115w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/3-Lemon-Zest-693x520.jpg 693w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/3-Lemon-Zest-391x293.jpg 391w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/3-Lemon-Zest-227x170.jpg 227w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/3-Lemon-Zest-500x375.jpg 500w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/3-Lemon-Zest-853x640.jpg 853w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/3-Lemon-Zest-150x113.jpg 150w" height="900" sizes="(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAP///wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw==" width="1200"/></figure>
<p><em>While the asparagus is roasting, zest one lemon. Youâll need about 1 tsp lemon zest. After zesting, cut the lemon into wedges.</em></p>
<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img alt="Lemon being squeezed on roasted asparagus" class="wp-image-54834" data-loading="lazy" data-pin-media="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/4-Lemon-on-Asparagus.jpg" data-src="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/4-Lemon-on-Asparagus.jpg" data-srcset="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/4-Lemon-on-Asparagus.jpg 1200w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/4-Lemon-on-Asparagus-400x300.jpg 400w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/4-Lemon-on-Asparagus-800x600.jpg 800w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/4-Lemon-on-Asparagus-347x260.jpg 347w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/4-Lemon-on-Asparagus-768x576.jpg 768w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/4-Lemon-on-Asparagus-115x86.jpg 115w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/4-Lemon-on-Asparagus-693x520.jpg 693w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/4-Lemon-on-Asparagus-391x293.jpg 391w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/4-Lemon-on-Asparagus-227x170.jpg 227w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/4-Lemon-on-Asparagus-500x375.jpg 500w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/4-Lemon-on-Asparagus-853x640.jpg 853w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/4-Lemon-on-Asparagus-150x113.jpg 150w" height="900" sizes="(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAP///wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw==" width="1200"/></figure>
<p><em>Roast the asparagus for about 20 minutes, or until they are browned to your liking (roasting time may vary depending on the girth of your asparagus). Stir the asparagus about halfway through roasting. Once roasted, add the lemon zest and a couple squeezes of lemon juice. Toss the asparagus to coat in lemon. Taste and adjust the salt or lemon to your liking.</em></p>
<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img alt="Lemon Garlic Rosted Asparagus on a sheet pan with lemon wedges" class="wp-image-54824" data-loading="lazy" data-pin-media="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/Lemon-Garlic-Roasted-Asparagus-pan.jpg" data-src="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/Lemon-Garlic-Roasted-Asparagus-pan.jpg" data-srcset="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/Lemon-Garlic-Roasted-Asparagus-pan.jpg 1200w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/Lemon-Garlic-Roasted-Asparagus-pan-400x300.jpg 400w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/Lemon-Garlic-Roasted-Asparagus-pan-800x600.jpg 800w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/Lemon-Garlic-Roasted-Asparagus-pan-347x260.jpg 347w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/Lemon-Garlic-Roasted-Asparagus-pan-768x576.jpg 768w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/Lemon-Garlic-Roasted-Asparagus-pan-115x86.jpg 115w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/Lemon-Garlic-Roasted-Asparagus-pan-693x520.jpg 693w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/Lemon-Garlic-Roasted-Asparagus-pan-391x293.jpg 391w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/Lemon-Garlic-Roasted-Asparagus-pan-227x170.jpg 227w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/Lemon-Garlic-Roasted-Asparagus-pan-500x375.jpg 500w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/Lemon-Garlic-Roasted-Asparagus-pan-853x640.jpg 853w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/03/Lemon-Garlic-Roasted-Asparagus-pan-150x113.jpg 150w" height="900" sizes="(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAP///wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw==" width="1200"/></figure>
<p><em>Serve the roasted asparagus with the remaining lemon wedges. Enjoy! And try not to eat the entire batch yourselfâ¦</em></p>

<div class="comment-content"><p>This recipe is for the tender green asparagus that are found in North America.  Iâve only seen the asparagus that need to be peeled in Germany.  These are white asparagus that are have a tougher skin that should be peeled first.</p>

<strong>Jim from Wixom</strong>            	 â
                <a href="https://www.budgetbytes.com/lemon-garlic-roasted-asparagus/comment-page-2/#comment-415878">

<a aria-label="Reply to Jim from Wixom" class="comment-reply-link" data-belowelement="comment-415878" data-commentid="415878" data-postid="13342" data-replyto="Reply to Jim from Wixom" data-respondelement="respond" href="#comment-415878" rel="nofollow">Reply</a> </div><!-- .comment-meta -->
<div class="comment-content"><p>Yes, this is very nice. I would like to add my own version if you like which Iâve made for the last 10 years. I only buy asparagus when it goes down to 1.99 / lb.  First the asparagus is marinated in olive oil, lemon juice and S&amp;P for a few hours. Then youâd fire up the grill and over medium heat lay out the asparagus. Cook until limp and darkened, some prefer black. Pick off the small ones as they will cook first and eat as the others cook. I try to buy only medium size stalks. Avoid the tiny thin ones as well as the large woody ones.  It should take 15 â 20 min. depending on the size of the veg. and your heat. A more gourmet version Iâve heard would be to wrap a few stalks in Prosciutto or Fontina cheese. Alternatively, you could just sprinkle your favorite cheese over the top on a serving dish and watch them dissapear.</p>
